               <div class="entry-wrapper">
                <h2 class="entry-title">
                 <a href="https://hongkongfp.com/2021/03/22/hong-kong-pro-beijing-group-claims-over-2-38-million-signatures-in-support-of-electoral-changes/" rel="bookmark">
                  Hong Kong pro-Beijing group claims over 2.38 million signatures in support of electoral changes
                 </a>
                </h2>
                <p>
                 A pro-Beijing group in Hong Kong claims it has gathered more than 2.38 million signatures in support of the looming electoral overhaul which aims to ensure that only “patriots” rule the city. The Sign For HK 2021 campaign – led by Beijing loyalist Tam Yiu-chung – announced on Sunday that more than 1.17 million people […]
                </p>
                <div class="entry-meta">
                 <a href="https://hongkongfp.com/author/kellyho/">
                  <amp-img alt="Kelly Ho" class="avatar avatar-48 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-48 alignnone photo amp-wp-enforced-sizes i-amphtml-layout-intrinsic i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" height="48" i-amphtml-layout="intrinsic" layout="intrinsic" src="https://hongkongfp.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/Kelly-2-Copy-100x100.jpg" width="48">
                   <i-amphtml-sizer class="i-amphtml-sizer">
                    <img alt="" aria-hidden="true" class="i-amphtml-intrinsic-sizer" role="presentation" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBoZWlnaHQ9JzQ4JyB3aWR0aD0nNDgnIHhtbG5zPSdodHRwOi8vd3d3LnczLm9yZy8yMDAwL3N2ZycgdmVyc2lvbj0nMS4xJy8+"/>
                   </i-amphtml-sizer>
                   <noscript>
                    <img alt="Kelly Ho" class="avatar avatar-48 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-48 alignnone photo" height="48" loading="lazy" src="https://hongkongfp.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/Kelly-2-Copy-100x100.jpg" width="48"/>
                   </noscript>

                 </a>

                  Protest innovations from Myanmar’s civil disobedience movement
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <p>
                 Myanmar’s military authorities have banned public assemblies but this has only encouraged protesters to devise new ways of expressing opposition to the coup. After the military grabbed power on February 1, a civil disobedience movement was launched which encouraged the public to stop going to work, boycott businesses owned by generals, and join anti-coup protests.       <section class="widget widget_text" id="text-2">
       <h2 class="widget-title">
        What is Hong Kong Free Press?
       </h2>
       <div class="textwidget">
        <p>
         Founded in 2015,
         <span class="amp-wp-f6bf23d" data-amp-original-style="text-decoration: underline;">
          <b>
           <a href="http://www.hongkongfp.com/about/">
            Hong Kong Free Press
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         is a non-profit, English-language newspaper – run by journalists and completely independent.
        </p>
        <p>
         HKFP is only answerable only to readers, not shareholders, media tycoons or corporate umbrella groups. Our work is governed by a
         <a href="https://www.hongkongfp.com/hkfp-code-ethics/">
          Code of Ethics
         </a>
         and we publish an
         <a href="https://hongkongfp.com/hong-kong-free-press-annual-report-2019/">
          Annual Report
         </a>
         and
         <a href="https://hongkongfp.com/hong-kong-free-press-transparency-report-2018/">
          Transparency Report
         </a>
         every year. Learn more about how you can
         <a href="http://www.hongkongfp.com/support-hkfp/">
          support us
         </a>
         and ensure our independence.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.ngosource.org/about-equivalency-determination-on-file-badge">
          <amp-img alt="NGO Source" class="alignnone wp-image-256235 amp-wp-enforced-sizes i-amphtml-layout-intrinsic i-amphtml-layout-size-defined" height="97" i-amphtml-layout="intrinsic" layout="intrinsic" src="https://hongkongfp-launch-performancetests.newspackstaging.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/NGO-Source.png" width="253">
           <i-amphtml-sizer class="i-amphtml-sizer">
            <img alt="" aria-hidden="true" class="i-amphtml-intrinsic-sizer" role="presentation" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBoZWlnaHQ9Jzk3JyB3aWR0aD0nMjUzJyB4bWxucz0naHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmcnIHZlcnNpb249JzEuMScvPg=="/>
           </i-amphtml-sizer>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="NGO Source" class="alignnone wp-image-256235" height="97" loading="lazy" src="https://hongkongfp-launch-performancetests.newspackstaging.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/NGO-Source.png" width="253"/>
           </noscript>
          </amp-img>
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
